SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[CategoryId], [s].[CompanyId], [s].[CreationTime], [s].[Description], [s].[ExpirationTime], [s].[ImageUrl], [s].[Name], [s].[Price], [s].[Quantity], [s].[Status], [s].[Id0], [s0].[Id], [s0].[CustomerId], [s0].[ProductOfferId], [s0].[PurchaseDate], [s0].[Quantity], [s0].[Status], [s0].[TotalPrice], [s0].[Id0], [s0].[Email], [s0].[Password], [s0].[Role], [s0].[UserName], [s0].[Balance], [s].[Email], [s].[Password], [s].[Role], [s].[UserName], [s].[Balance], [s].[ImageUrl0], [s].[IsActivated]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CompanyId], [p].[CreationTime], [p].[Description], [p].[ExpirationTime], [p].[ImageUrl], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [p].[Quantity], [p].[Status], [u0].[Id] AS [Id0], [u0].[Email], [u0].[Password], [u0].[Role], [u0].[UserName], [u0].[Balance], [u0].[ImageUrl] AS [ImageUrl0], [u0].[IsActivated]
    FROM [ProductOffers] AS [p]
    INNER JOIN (
        SELECT [u].[Id], [u].[Email], [u].[Password], [u].[Role], [u].[UserName], [u].[Balance], [u].[ImageUrl], [u].[IsActivated]
        FROM [Users] AS [u]
        WHERE [u].[Role] = 1
    ) AS [u0] ON [p].[CompanyId] = [u0].[Id]
    WHERE [p].[Id] = @__offerId_0 AND [p].[CompanyId] = @__companyId_1 AND [p].[Status] = 0
) AS [s]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[Id], [p0].[CustomerId], [p0].[ProductOfferId], [p0].[PurchaseDate], [p0].[Quantity], [p0].[Status], [p0].[TotalPrice], [u2].[Id] AS [Id0], [u2].[Email], [u2].[Password], [u2].[Role], [u2].[UserName], [u2].[Balance]
    FROM [Purchases] AS [p0]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [u1].[Id], [u1].[Email], [u1].[Password], [u1].[Role], [u1].[UserName], [u1].[Balance]
        FROM [Users] AS [u1]
        WHERE [u1].[Role] = 2
    ) AS [u2] ON [p0].[CustomerId] = [u2].[Id]
